   if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\\\\n      goBack();\\\\n      return;\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // Step-specific commands\\\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\\\n      // Extract digits for phone\\\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\\\n      if (digits.length >= 3) {\\\\n        voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\\\n        return;\\\\n      }\\\\n      // Confirmation\\\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\\\\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\\\n          goToStep('otp', 'Verification');\\\\n          voice.speak(\\\\\\\"Sending verification code now. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\\\\\");\\\\n        }\\\\n        return;\\\\n      }\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    if (step === 'otp') {\\\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\\\n      if (digits.length >= 1) {\\\\n        voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\\\n        return;\\\\n      }\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\\\n      // Let profile component handle it\\\\n      if (voiceCommandHandlerRef.current?.(cmd)) {\\\\n        return;\\\\n      }\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\\\\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('go live')) {\\\\n        goToStep('upload', 'Upload');\\\\n        voice.speak(\\\\\\\"Great! '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6', 'sex': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9',\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\s,.\\-]+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\n  }\n  // Also try raw digits\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const w: Record<string, string> = VISTAVIEW - VENDOR PHONE v2.0 (ORIGINAL)\n// Voice-first phone capture with digit extraction\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface VendorPhoneProps {\n  value: string;\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\n  onNext: () => void;\n  speak: (text: string) => void;\n  onVoiceDigits?: (handler: (digits: string) => void) => void;\n}\n\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\n// Format phone as 703-338-4931\nconst formatPhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\n// Speak phone as \"seven zero three \u2014 three three eight \u2014 four nine three one\"\nconst speakablePhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  const words: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  const digitWords = clean.split('').map(d => words[d] || d);\n  \n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\n    return `${digitWords.slice(0, 3).join(' ')} \u2014 ${digitWords.slice(3, 6).join(' ')} \u2014 ${digitWords.slice(6, 10).join(' ')}`;\n  }\n  return digitWords.join(' ');\n};\n\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<VendorPhoneProps> = ({ \n  value, \n  onChange, \n  onNext, \n  speak,\n  onVoiceDigits \n}) => {\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(value);\n  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false);\n  const [awaitingConfirmation, setAwaitingConfirmation] = useState(false);\n\n  // Update phone from parent value\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (value && value !== phone.replace(/-/g, '')) {\n      setPhone(formatPhone(value));\n    }\n  }, [value]);\n\n  // Handle voice digits\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    // Append new digits to existing\n    const currentDigits = phone.replace(/-/g, '');\n    const newDigits = (currentDigits + digits).slice(0, 10);\n    const newPhone = formatPhone(newDigits);\n    \n    setPhone(newPhone);\n    onChange(newDigits);\n    \n    if (newDigits.length >= 10) {\n      // Ask for confirmation\n      setAwaitingConfirmation(true);\n      speak(`I heard: ${speakablePhone(newDigits)}. Is that correct? Say \"yes\" to confirm or \"no\" to re-enter.`);\n    } else if (digits.length > 0) {\n      // Acknowledge partial entry\n      speak(digits.split('').join(' '));\n    }\n  }, [phone, onChange, speak]);\n\n  // Register voice digit handler\n  useEffect(() => {\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\n\n  // Handle typed input\n  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const digits = e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    const formatted = formatPhone(digits);\n    setPhone(formatted);\n    onChange(digits);\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\n    setConfirmed(false);\n  };\n\n  // Handle confirmation\n  const handleConfirm = () => {\n    setConfirmed(true);\n    speak(`Perfect! Sending verification code to ${speakablePhone(phone.replace(/-/g, ''))}. For demo, use code 1 2 3 4 5 6.`);\n    setTimeout(onNext, 2000);\n  };\n\n  // Clear phone\n  const handleClear = () => {\n    setPhone('');\n    onChange('');\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\n    setConfirmed(false);\n    speak(\"Cleared. '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst STEPS = [\n  { id: 1, label: 'Parsing catalog structure', icon: '\ud83d\udccb', duration: 2000 },\n  { id: 2, label: 'Extracting images', icon: duration = STEPS[stepIdx].duration;\n        const startProgress = (stepIdx / STEPS.length) * 100;\n        const endProgress = ((stepIdx + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100;\n        const startTime = Date.now();\n        \n        const animate = () => {\n          const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;\n          const p = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);\n          setProgress(startProgress + (endProgress - startProgress) * p);\n          \n          if (p < 1) {\n            requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n          } else {\n            stepIdx++;\n            setTimeout(runStep, VISTAVIEW - VENDOR PHONE v2.0 (ORIGINAL)\\n// Voice-first phone capture with digit extraction\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface VendorPhoneProps {\\n  value: string;\\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\\n  onNext: () => void;\\n  speak: (text: string) => void;\\n  onVoiceDigits?: (handler: (digits: string) => void) => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\n// Format phone as 703-338-4931\\nconst formatPhone = (digits: string): string => {\\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\n// Speak phone as \\\"seven zero three \\u2014 three three eight \\u2014 four nine three one\\\"\\nconst speakablePhone = (digits: string): string => {\\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  const words: Record<string, string> = {\\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\\n  };\\n  const digitWords = clean.split('').map(d => words[d] || d);\\n  \\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\\n    return `${digitWords.slice(0, 3).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${digitWords.slice(3, 6).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${digitWords.slice(6, 10).join(' ')}`;\\n  }\\n  return digitWords.join(' ');\\n};\\n\\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<VendorPhoneProps> = ({ \\n  value, \\n  onChange, \\n  onNext, \\n  speak,\\n  onVoiceDigits \\n}) => {\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(value);\\n  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false);\\n  const [awaitingConfirmation, setAwaitingConfirmation] = useState(false);\\n\\n  // Update phone from parent value\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (value && value !== phone.replace(/-/g, '')) {\\n      setPhone(formatPhone(value));\\n    }\\n  }, [value]);\\n\\n  // Handle voice digits\\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    // Append new digits to existing\\n    const currentDigits = phone.replace(/-/g, '');\\n    const newDigits = (currentDigits + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n    const newPhone = formatPhone(newDigits);\\n    \\n    setPhone(newPhone);\\n    onChange(newDigits);\\n    \\n    if (newDigits.length >= 10) {\\n      // Ask for confirmation\\n      setAwaitingConfirmation(true);\\n      speak(`I heard: ${speakablePhone(newDigits)}. Is that correct? Say \\\"yes\\\" to confirm or \\\"no\\\" to re-enter.`);\\n    } else if (digits.length > 0) {\\n      // Acknowledge partial entry\\n      speak(digits.split('').join(' '));\\n    }\\n  }, [phone, onChange, speak]);\\n\\n  // Register voice digit handler\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\\n\\n  // Handle typed input\\n  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\\n    const digits = e.target.value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    const formatted = formatPhone(digits);\\n    setPhone(formatted);\\n    onChange(digits);\\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\\n    setConfirmed(false);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle confirmation\\n  const handleConfirm = () => {\\n    setConfirmed(true);\\n    speak(`Perfect! Sending verification code to ${speakablePhone(phone.replace(/-/g, ''))}. For demo, use code 1 2 3 4 5 6.`);\\n    setTimeout(onNext, 2000);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Clear phone\\n  const handleClear = () => {\\n    setPhone('');\\n    onChange('');\\n    setAwaitingConfirmation(false);\\n    setConfirmed(false);\\n    speak(\\\"Cleared. \\ud83d\\udcc4\\n            </div>\\n            <div style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: 'left' }}>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontWeight: 500 }}>{selectedFile.name}</p>\\n \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface VendorPipelineProps {\\n  fileName?: string;\\n  onComplete: () => void;\\n  speak: (text: string) => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst STEPS = [\\n  { id: 1, label: 'Parsing catalog structure', icon: '\\ud83d\\udccb', duration: 2000 },\\n  { id: 2, label: 'Extracting images', icon: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', duration: 2500 },\\n  { id: 3, label: 'Enhancing image quality', icon: '\\u2728', duration: 3000 },\\n  { id: 4, label: 'Creating product tables', icon: '\\ud83d\\udcca', duration: 2000 },\\n  { id: 5, label: 'Publishing to catalog', icon: '\\ud83d\\ude80', duration: 1500 }\\n];\\n\\nconst VendorPipeline: React.FC<VendorPipelineProps> = ({ fileName, onComplete, speak }) => {\\n  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(0);\\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    speak(\\\"Starting the 5-step processing pipeline.\\\");\\n    \\n    let stepIdx = 0;\\n    const runStep = () => {\\n      if (stepIdx < STEPS.length) {\\n        setCurrentStep(stepIdx + 1);\\n        speak(STEPS[stepIdx].label);\\n        \\n        // Animate progress\\n        const duration = STEPS[stepIdx].duration;\\n        const startProgress = (stepIdx / STEPS.length) * 100;\\n        const endProgress = ((stepIdx + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100;\\n        const startTime = Date.now();\\n        \\n        const animate = () => {\\n          const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;\\n          const p = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);\\n          setProgress(startProgress + (endProgress - startProgress) * p);\\n          \\n          if (p < 1) {\\n            requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n          } else {\\n            stepIdx++;\\n            setTimeout(runStep, 500);\\n          }\\n        };\\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n      } else {\\n        setTimeout(onComplete, 500);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    setTimeout(runStep, 1000);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\u2699\\ufe0f</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\\n        Processing Your Catalog\\n      </h3>\\n      {fileName && (\\n        <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\\n          {fileName}\\n        </p>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Progress Bar */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n        borderRadius: '10px',\\n        height: '20px',\\n        marginBottom: '24px',\\n        overflow: 'hidden'\\n      }}>\\n        <div style={{\\n          background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${THEME.gold}, ${THEME.goldLight})`,\\n          height: '100%',\\n          width: `${progress}%`,\\n          borderRadius: '10px',\\n          transition: 'width 0.1s linear'\\n        }} />\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Steps */}\\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'left', maxWidth: '400px', margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n        {STEPS.map((step, idx) => {\\n          const isComplete = currentStep > step.id;\\n          const isCurrent = currentStep === step.id;\\n          \\n          return (\\n            <div key={step.id} style={{\\n              display: 'flex',\\n              alignItems: 'center',\\n              gap: '12px',\\n              padding: '12px 16px',\\n              background: isCurrent ? 'rgba(184,134,11,0.15)' : 'transparent',\\n              borderRadius: '10px',\\n              marginBottom: '8px',\\n              transition: 'all 0.3s'\\n            }}>\\n              <div style={{\\n                width: '32px',\\n                height: '32px',\\n                borderRadius: '50%',\\n                background: isComplete ? '#4CAF50' : isCurrent ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n                display: 'flex',\\n                alignItems: 'center',\\n                justifyContent: 'center',\\n                fontSize: isComplete ? '1em' : '1.2em'\\n              }}>\\n                {isComplete ? '\\u2713' : step.icon}\\n              </div>\\n              <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>\\n                <div style={{ \\n                  color: isComplete ? '#4CAF50' : isCurrent ? '#fff' : '#666',\\n                  fontWeight: isCurrent ? 600 : 400\\n                }}>\\n                  {step.label}\\n                </div>\\n              </div>\\n              {isCurrent && (\\n                <div style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, fontSize: '0.8em' }}>\\n                  Processing...\\n                </div>\\n              )}\\n            </div>\\n          );\\n        })}\\n      </div>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VendorPipeline;\\nVENDORPIPELINEEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 VendorPipeline.tsx restored\\\"\\n\\n# Global commands\\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || goBack();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific commands\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      // Extract digits for phone\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\n      if (digits.length >= 3) {\\n        voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      // Confirmation\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\n          goToStep('otp', 'Verification');\\n          voice.speak(\\\"Sending verification code now. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\");\\n        }\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'otp') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\n      if (digits.length >= 1) {\\n        voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('next')) {\\n        goToStep('dashboard', 'Dashboard');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved! Welcome to your Vendor Dashboard.\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('beautify') || cmd.includes('enhance')) {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Enhancing your profile with AI...\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('go live')) {\\n        goToStep('upload', 'Upload');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Great! Upload your catalog. I'll process it and publish your products.\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'complete') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\\n        onComplete();\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\\n        onClose();\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // Handle voice digits\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    voiceDigitHandlerRef.current?.(digits);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const voice = useVoice({ \\n    onCommand: handleCommand, \\n    onDigits: handleDigits,\\n    autoStart: isOpen \\n  });\\n\\n  // Go back to previous step\\n  const goBack = () => {\\n    const stepOrder: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\\n    const idx = stepOrder.indexOf(step);\\n    \\n    if (idx === 0) {\\n      onBack(); // Go back to role selection\\n    } else {\\n      const prev = stepOrder[idx - 1];\\n      setStep(prev);\\n      navStack.pop();\\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label || prev}.`);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Go to specific step\\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step, label: string) => {\\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label });\\n    setStep(newStep);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Welcome message on open\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Welcome, Vendor! updated)\n  - Recoverable from backup\n```\n\n### RULE 8: SINGLE MIC RULE\n```\nOnly ONE voice interface at a time:\n  - Landing page OR modal OR dashboard\n  - When modal opens \u2192 pause main RULE: Digit extraction from VV-AS-v1.0.json\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9',\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\s,.\\-]+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    } else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) {\n      digits += word;\n    }\n  }\n  // Also extract raw digits\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  const words = clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x);\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\n    return `${words.slice(0,3).join(' ')} \u2014 ${words.slice(3,6).join(' ')} \u2014 ${words.slice(6,10).join(' ')}`;\n  }\n  return words.join(' ');\n};\n\nexport const useVoice = ({ onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true }: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\n\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition STARTED');\n      setIsListening(true);\n      retryCountRef.current = 0;\n    };\n\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\n\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      \n      console.log('[useVoice] Heard:', text, 'Final:', result.isFinal);\n      \n      if (text) {\n        setTranscript(text);\n      }\n\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\n        \n        // Extract and pass digits FIRST (for phone/OTP)\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\n        if (digits.length > 0) {\n          console.log('[useVoice] Extracted digits:', digits);\n          digitsRef.current?.(digits);\n        }\n        \n        // Then pass full command\n        commandRef.current?.(cmd);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'no-speech' || event.error === 'aborted') {\n        // Normal - just restart\n      } else if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        console.error('[useVoice] Microphone access denied');\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended, isActive:', isActiveRef.current);\n      if (isActiveRef.current && retryCountRef.current < 50) {\n        retryCountRef.current++;\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          try {\n            recognition.start();\n          } catch (e) {\n            console.log('[useVoice] Restart failed, retrying...');\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n   setIsPaused(false);\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\n    try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  return {\n    isListening,\n    isSpeaking,\n    isPaused,\n    transcript,\n \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\n// RULE: Digit extraction from VV-AS-v1.0.json\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\\n  'five': '5',\\n  'six': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9',\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\\\s,.\\\\-]+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    } else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) {\\n      digits += word;\\n    }\\n  }\\n  // Also extract raw digits\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\\n  };\\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  const words = clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x);\\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\\n    return `${words.slice(0,3).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${words.slice(3,6).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${words.slice(6,10).join(' ')}`;\\n  }\\n  return words.join(' ');\\n};\\n\\nexport const useVoice = ({ onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true }: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\\n\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\\n  const commandRef = useRef(onCommand);\\n  const digitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\\n  const retryCountRef = useRef(0);\\n\\n  // Keep refs updated\\n  useEffect(() => { commandRef.current = onCommand; }, [onCommand]);\\n  useEffect(() => { digitsRef.current = onDigits; }, [onDigits]);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech synthesis\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    // Preload voices\\n    const loadVoices = () => synthRef.current?.getVoices();\\n    loadVoices();\\n    window.speechSynthesis?.addEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\\n    return () => window.speechSynthesis?.removeEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech recognition - THIS IS THE FIX\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n\\n    const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SpeechRecognition) {\\n      console.warn('[useVoice] Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\\n    recognition.continuous = true;\\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\\n\\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition STARTED');\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n      retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\\n\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      \\n      console.log('[useVoice] Heard:', text, 'Final:', result.isFinal);\\n      \\n      if (text) {\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n      }\\n\\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\\n        \\n        // Extract and pass digits FIRST (for phone/OTP)\\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n        if (digits.length > 0) {\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Extracted digits:', digits);\\n          digitsRef.current?.(digits);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Then pass full command\\n        commandRef.current?.(cmd);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'no-speech' || event.error === 'aborted') {\\n        // Normal - just restart\\n      } else if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        console.error('[useVoice] Microphone access denied');\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended, isActive:', isActiveRef.current);\\n      if (isActiveRef.current && retryCountRef.current < 50) {\\n        retryCountRef.current++;\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          try {\\n            recognition.start();\\n          } catch (e) {\\n            console.log('[useVoice] Restart failed, retrying...');\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recRef.current = recognition;\\n\\n    // AUTO-START if requested\\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Auto-starting recognition...');\\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\\n      // Small delay to ensure component is mounted\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        try {\\n          recognition.start();\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Recognition start() called');\\n        } catch (e) {\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Start failed, will retry');\\n        }\\n      }, 300);\\n    }\\n\\n    return () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Cleanup - stopping recognition');\\n      isActiveRef.current = false;\\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n    };\\n  }, [autoStart]);\\n\\n  const synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n\\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices[0];\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n\\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Done speaking');\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    };\\n    utterance.onerror = () => const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] startListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.start();\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Already started or error');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] stopListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.stop();\\n    } catch (e) {}\\n    setIsListening(false);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\\n    setIsPaused(true);\\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  return {\\n    isListening,\\n    isSpeaking,\\n    isPaused,\\n    transcript,\\n    displayText,\\n    speak,\\n    stop,\\n    startListening,\\n    stopListening,\\n    pause,\\n    resume,\\n    // Export utilities for components\\n    extractDigits,\\n    formatPhoneNumber,\\n go to previous\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\n    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) {\n      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Handle paste\n  const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    const pasted = e.clipboardData.getData('text').replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6);\n    if (pasted.length > 0) {\n      const newOtp = [...otp];\n      for (let i = 0; i < pasted.length; i++) {\n        newOtp[i] = pasted[i];\n      }\n      setOtp(newOtp);\n      if (pasted.length === 6) {\n        setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(pasted), 300);\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Verify OTP\n  const verifyOTP = (code: string) => {\n    if (verifying || verified) return;\n    \n    setVerifying(true);\n    speak(\"Verifying code...\");\n    \n    setTimeout(() => {\n      if (code === DEMO_OTP) {\n        setVerified(true);\n        speak(\"Code verified! Welcome aboard!\");\n        setTimeout(onVerified, 1500);\n      } else {\n        setError('Incorrect code. Use 123456 for demo.');\n        speak(\"That code is incorrect. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        setVerifying(false);\n        // Clear and focus first\n        setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n        inputRefs.current[0]?.focus();\n      }\n    }, 1000);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n        Enter Verification Code\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '8px', fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\n        Sent to <strong style={{ color: '#fff' }}>{phone}</strong>\n      </p>\n      <p style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\n        Demo code: <strong style={{ color: THEME.goldLight }}>1 2 3 4 5 6</strong>\n      </p>\n\n      {/* OTP Input Boxes */}\n      <div style={{ \n        display: 'flex', \n        justifyContent: 'center', \n        gap: '10px', \n        marginBottom: '20px' \n      }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, index) => (\n          <input\n            key={index}\n            ref={(el) => { inputRefs.current[index] = el; }}\n            type=\"text\"\n            inputMode=\"numeric\"\n            maxLength={1}\n            value={digit}\n            onChange={(e) => handleChange(index, e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(index, e)}\n            onPaste={index === 0 ? handlePaste : undefined}\n            disabled={verifying || verified}\n            autoFocus={index === 0}\n            style={{\n              width: '50px',\n              height: '60px',\n              fontSize: '1.8em',\n              textAlign: 'center',\n              borderRadius: '12px',\n              border: `2px solid ${error ? '#e74c3c' : digit ? '#4CAF50' : THEME.gold}`,\n              background: digit ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.1)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontWeight: 600,\n              outline: 'none',\n              transition: 'all 0.2s'\n            }}\n          />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Error */}\n      {error && (\n        <p style={{ color: '#e74c3c', fontSize: '0.9em', marginBottom: '16px' }}>\n          \u26a0\ufe0f {error}\n        </p>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Status */}\n      {verifying && !verified && (\n        <div style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '16px' }}>\n          \u23f3 Verifying...\n        </div>\n      )}\n      {verified && (\n        <div style={{ color: '#4CAF50', marginBottom: '16px', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>\n          \u2713 Verified! Continuing...\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Resend */}\n      {!verified && !verifying && (\n        <button\n          onClick={() => speak(\"A new code has been sent.\")}\n          style={{\n            background: 'transparent',\n            border: 'none',\n            color: THEME.gold,\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            textDecoration: 'underline',\n            fontSize: '0.9em'\n          }}\n        >\n          Resend Code\n        </button>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Voice hint */}\n      <p style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.8em', marginTop: '20px' }}>\n        \ud83d\udca1 Say: \"one two three four five six\"\n      </p>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VendorOTP;\nVENDOROTPEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 VendorOTP.tsx FIXED\"\n\n# go to previous\\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\\n    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) {\\n      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle paste\\n  const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    const pasted = e.clipboardData.getData('text').replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6);\\n    if (pasted.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = [...otp];\\n      for (let i = 0; i < pasted.length; i++) {\\n        newOtp[i] = pasted[i];\\n      }\\n      setOtp(newOtp);\\n      if (pasted.length === 6) {\\n        setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(pasted), 300);\\n      }\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Verify OTP\\n  const verifyOTP = (code: string) => {\\n    if (verifying || verified) return;\\n    \\n    setVerifying(true);\\n    speak(\\\"Verifying code...\\\");\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      if (code === DEMO_OTP) {\\n        setVerified(true);\\n        speak(\\\"Code verified! '#e74c3c' : digit ? '#4CAF50' : THEME.gold}`,\\n              background: digit ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.1)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n              color: '#fff',\\n              fontWeight: 600,\\n              outline: 'none',\\n              transition: 'all 0.2s'\\n            }}\\n          />\\n        ))}\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Error */}\\n      {error && (\\n        <p style={{ color: '#e74c3c', fontSize: '0.9em', marginBottom: '16px' }}>\\n          \\u26a0\\ufe0f {error}\\n        </p>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Status */}\\n      {verifying && !verified && (\\n        <div style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '16px' }}>\\n          \\u23f3 Verifying...\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n      {verified && (\\n        <div style={{ color: '#4CAF50', marginBottom: '16px', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>\\n          \\u2713 Verified! '../common/useVoice';\nimport { useNavStack } from '../common/useNavStack';\nimport VendorPhone from './VendorPhone';\nimport VendorOTP from './VendorOTP';\nimport VendorProfile from './VendorProfile';\nimport VendorDashboard from './VendorDashboard';\nimport VendorUpload from './VendorUpload';\nimport VendorPipeline from './VendorPipeline';\n\ninterface VendorFlowProps {\n STEPS: { id: Step; label: string }[] = [\n  { id: 'phone', label: 'Phone' },\n  { id: 'otp', label: 'Verify' },\n  { id: 'profile', label: 'Profile' },\n  { id: 'dashboard', label: 'Dashboard' },\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\n];\n\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\n    phone: '',\n    vendorId: '',\n    profile: '',\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\n    companyName: '',\n    catalogFile: null as File | null,\n    products: [] as any[]\n  });\n\n  // CRITICAL: Refs to pass voice digits to child components\n  const voiceDigitHandlerRef = useRef<((digits: string) => void) | null>(null);\n\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone' });\n\n  // Voice command handler\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd);\n    \n    // Global commands\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\n      voice.stop();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || cmd.includes('cancel')) {\n      voice.stop();\n      onClose();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\n      goBack();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Phone\n    if (step === 'phone') {\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\n          goToStep('otp');\n          voice.speak(\"Sending code. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Profile\n    if (step === 'profile') {\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('next')) {\n        saveProfile();\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('beautify') || cmd.includes('enhance')) {\n        voice.speak(\"Enhancing your profile with AI...\");\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Dashboard\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\n        goToStep('upload');\n        voice.speak(\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\");\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Complete\n    if (step === 'complete') {\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\n        onComplete();\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\n        onClose();\n      }\n    }\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\n\n  // CRITICAL: Voice digit handler - passes to child components\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Received digits:', digits, 'Current step:', step);\n    // Pass to the registered handler (VendorPhone or VendorOTP)\n    if (voiceDigitHandlerRef.current) {\n      voiceDigitHandlerRef.current(digits);\n    }\n  }, [step]);\n\n  const voice = useVoice({ \n    onCommand: handleCommand, \n    onDigits: handleDigits,\n    autoStart: isOpen \n  });\n\n  // Navigation\n  const goBack = () => {\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx <= 0) {\n      onBack();\n    } else {\n      const prev = order[idx - 1];\n      setStep(prev);\n      navStack.pop();\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\n    setStep(newStep);\n  };\n\n  // Save profile to backend\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\n    voice.speak(\"Saving your profile...\");\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say 'upload catalog' to add products.\");\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved locally. Say 'upload catalog' to continue.\");\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Welcome on open\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        voice.speak(\"Welcome, Vendor! Let's set you up. Tell me your phone number. Say each digit clearly.\");\n      }, 500);\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  // Cleanup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!isOpen) {\n      voice.stop();\n      voice.stopListening();\n      setStep('phone');\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ \n      position: 'fixed', inset: 0, \n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', \n      zIndex: 10000, \n      display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', \n      padding: '20px' \n    }}>\n      <div style={{ \n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, \n        borderRadius: '20px', \n        width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', \n        overflow: 'hidden', \n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`,\n        display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column'\n      }}>\n        \n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{ \n          padding: '16px 24px', \n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, \n          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' \n        }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n            <div>\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)'\n            }} />\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Agent Bar */}\n        <AgentBar\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\n          onStop={voice.stop}\n          onPause={voice.pause}\n          onResume={voice.resume}\n          onBack={goBack}\n          onClose={onClose}\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\n          showModes={true}\n          showNavButtons={true}\n        />\n\n        {/* Content */}\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\n          \n          {step === 'phone' && (\n            <VendorPhone\n              value={vendorData.phone}\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\n              onNext={() => {\n                goToStep('otp');\n                voice.speak(`Sending code to ${speakablePhone(vendorData.phone)}. You can browse the homepage while I work. I'll notify you when done.`);\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\n            <VendorPipeline\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\n              vendorId={vendorData.vendorId}\n              onComplete={(products) => {\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\n                setStep('complete');\n                voice.speak(\"Congratulations! Your catalog is live on VistaView!\");\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onBrowseHome={() => {\n                voice.speak(\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing and notify you when done.\");\n                // Could minimize modal here\n              }}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'complete' && (\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\n              <div style={{ \n                width: '100px', height: '100px', borderRadius: '50%', \n                background: \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport '../common/useVoice';\\nimport { useNavStack } from '../common/useNavStack';\\nimport VendorPhone from './VendorPhone';\\nimport VendorOTP from './VendorOTP';\\nimport VendorProfile from label: 'Dashboard' },\\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\\n];\\n\\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\\n    phone: '',\\n    vendorId: '',\\n    profile: '',\\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\\n    companyName: '',\\n    catalogFile: null as File | null,\\n    products: [] as any[]\\n  });\\n\\n  // CRITICAL: Refs to pass voice digits to child components\\n  const voiceDigitHandlerRef = useRef<((digits: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n\\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone' });\\n\\n  // Voice command handler\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd);\\n    \\n    // Global commands\\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || cmd.includes('cancel')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      onClose();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\\n      goBack();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Phone\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\n          goToStep('otp');\\n          voice.speak(\\\"Sending code. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\");\\n        }\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Profile\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('next')) {\\n        saveProfile();\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('beautify') || cmd.includes('enhance')) {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Enhancing your profile with AI...\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Dashboard\\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\\n        goToStep('upload');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Complete\\n    if (step === 'complete') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\\n        onComplete();\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\\n        onClose();\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // CRITICAL: Voice digit handler - passes to child components\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Received digits:', digits, 'Current step:', step);\\n    // Pass to the registered handler (VendorPhone or VendorOTP)\\n    if (voiceDigitHandlerRef.current) {\\n      voiceDigitHandlerRef.current(digits);\\n    }\\n  }, [step]);\\n\\n  const voice = useVoice({ \\n    onCommand: handleCommand, \\n    onDigits: handleDigits,\\n    autoStart: isOpen \\n  });\\n\\n  // Navigation\\n  const goBack = () => {\\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx <= 0) {\\n      onBack();\\n    } else {\\n      const prev = order[idx - 1];\\n      setStep(prev);\\n      navStack.pop();\\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\\n    setStep(newStep);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Save profile to backend\\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\\n    voice.speak(\\\"Saving your profile...\\\");\\n    try {\\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({\\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\\n        })\\n      });\\n      const data = await res.json();\\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say 'upload catalog' to add products.\\\");\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved locally. Say 'upload catalog' to continue.\\\");\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Welcome on open\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Welcome, Vendor! Let's set you up. Tell me your phone number. Say each digit clearly.\\\");\\n      }, 500);\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  // Cleanup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!isOpen) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      voice.stopListening();\\n      setStep('phone');\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\\n\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ \\n      position: 'fixed', inset: 0, \\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', \\n      zIndex: 10000, \\n      display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', \\n      padding: '20px' \\n    }}>\\n      <div style={{ \\n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, \\n        borderRadius: '20px', \\n        width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', \\n        overflow: 'hidden', \\n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`,\\n        display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column'\\n      }}>\\n        \\n        {/* Header */}\\n        <div style={{ \\n          padding: '16px 24px', \\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, \\n          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' \\n        }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\\ud83d\\udce6</span>\\n            <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\\n            </div>\\n          </div>\\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{\\n            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff',\\n            width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em'\\n          }}>\\u2715</button>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: '4px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ \\n              flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', \\n              background: stepIndex >= i ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)'\\n            }} />\\n          ))}\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Agent Bar */}\\n        <AgentBar\\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\\n          onStop={voice.stop}\\n          onPause={voice.pause}\\n          onResume={voice.resume}\\n          onBack={goBack}\\n          onClose={onClose}\\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\\n          showModes={true}\\n          showNavButtons={true}\\n        />\\n\\n        {/* Content */}\\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\\n          \\n          {step === 'phone' && (\\n            <VendorPhone\\n              value={vendorData.phone}\\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\\n              onNext={() => {\\n                goToStep('otp');\\n                voice.speak(`Sending code to ${speakablePhone(vendorData.phone)}. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.`);\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'otp' && (\\n            <VendorOTP\\n              phone={formatPhoneNumber(vendorData.phone)}\\n              onVerified={() => {\\n                goToStep('profile');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Verified! Now tell me about your business.\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'profile' && (\\n            <VendorProfile\\n              profile={vendorData.profile}\\n              beautified={vendorData.beautifiedProfile}\\n              companyName={vendorData.companyName}\\n              onChange={(profile) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, profile }))}\\n              onCompanyChange={(name) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, companyName: name }))}\\n              onBeautify={(b) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, beautifiedProfile: b }))}\\n              onSave={saveProfile}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'dashboard' && (\\n            <VendorDashboard\\n              vendorName={vendorData.companyName || 'Your Store'}\\n              onUploadCatalog={() => {\\n                goToStep('upload');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. I'll process it and publish your products.\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'upload' && (\\n            <VendorUpload\\n              onFileSelected={(file) => {\\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, catalogFile: file }));\\n                goToStep('pipeline');\\n                voice.speak(`Processing ${file.name}. You can browse the homepage while I work. I'll notify you when done.`);\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\\n            <VendorPipeline\\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\\n              vendorId={vendorData.vendorId}\\n              onComplete={(products) => {\\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\\n                setStep('complete');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Congratulations! Your catalog is live on VistaView!\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onBrowseHome={() => {\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing and notify you when done.\\\");\\n                // Could minimize modal here\\n              }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'complete' && (\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\\n              <div style={{ \\n                width: '100px', height: '100px', borderRadius: '50%', \\n                background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #4CAF50, #2E7D32)', \\n                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',\\n                margin: '0 auto 24px', boxShadow: '0 0 30px THEME.gold, marginBottom: '12px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n                \\ud83c\\udf89 You're Live on VistaView!\\n              </h3>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#aaa', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\\n                {vendorData.products?.length || 0} products published\\n              </p>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: '32px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n                Find your store in Product Catalogue\\n              </p>\\n              \\n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>\\n                <button onClick={onComplete} style={{ \\n                  padding: '14px 32px', background: THEME.gold, color: '#000', \\n                  border: 'none', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer',           padding: '14px 24px', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', color: '#fff', \\n                  border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}`, borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer'\\n string) => void;\\n  onBeautify: (beautified: string) => void;\\n  onSave: () => void;\\n  speak: (text: string) => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\n// LinkedIn-style beautification templates\\nconst beautifyProfile = (raw: string, company: string): string => {\\n  const lines = raw.split('\\\\n').filter(l => l.trim());\\n  const bullets = VendorProfile: React.FC<Props> = ({\\n  profile, beautified, companyName,\\n  onChange, onCompanyChange, onBeautify, onSave, speak\\n}) => {\\n  const [isBeautifying, setIsBeautifying] = return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\\n    speak(\\\"Enhancing your profile LinkedIn style...\\\");\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      const enhanced = beautifyProfile(profile, Identifying tables, headers, and product listings.\\\" },\\n  { id: 2, label: 'Extracting product images', icon: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', duration: 3000,\\n    narration: \\\"Step 2: Extracting product images. Found multiple images, processing each one.\\\" },\\n  { id: 3, label: 'Enhancing image quality', icon: '\\u2728', duration: 3500,\\n    narration: \\\"Step 3: Enhancing image quality with AI. Improving resolution and color balance.\\\" },\\n  { id: 4, label: 'Creating product database', icon: '\\ud83d\\udcca', duration: 2500,\\n    narration: \\\"Step 4: Creating product database entries. Adding titles, descriptions, and prices.\\\" },\\n  { id: 5, label: 'Publishing to catalog', icon: '\\ud83d\\ude80', duration: 2000,\\n    narration: \\\"Step 5: Publishing to VistaView catalog. Almost done!\\\" }\\n];\\n\\nconst VendorPipeline: React.FC<Props> = ({ fileName, vendorId, onComplete, speak, onBrowseHome }) => {\\n  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(0);\\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\\n  const [statusText, setStatusText] = useState('Initializing...');\\n  const [canBrowse, setCanBrowse] = useState(false);\\n  const isMountedRef = useRef(true);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    isMountedRef.current = true;\\n    \\n    // Initial narration\\n    speak(\\\"Starting the 5-step processing pipeline. I'll narrate each step.\\\");\\n    \\n    let stepIdx = 0;\\n    \\n    const runStep = () => {\\n      if (!isMountedRef.current) return;\\n      \\n      if (stepIdx < STEPS.length) {\\n        const step = STEPS[stepIdx];\\n        setCurrentStep(stepIdx + 1);\\n        setStatusText(step.label);\\n        \\n        // SPEAK the step narration\\n        speak(step.narration);\\n        \\n        // Enable browse option after step 2\\n        if (stepIdx >= 1) {\\n          setCanBrowse(true);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Animate progress\\n        const startProgress = (stepIdx / STEPS.length) * 100;\\n        const endProgress = ((stepIdx + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100;\\n        const startTime = Date.now();\\n        \\n        const animate = () => {\\n          if (!isMountedRef.current) return;\\n          const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;\\n          const p = Math.min(elapsed / step.duration, 1);\\n          setProgress(startProgress + (endProgress - startProgress) * p);\\n          \\n          if (p < 1) {\\n            requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n          } else {\\n            stepIdx++;\\n            setTimeout(runStep, 800);\\n          }\\n        };\\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n      } else {\\n        // All done\\n        speak(\\\"Processing complete! Your products are now live.\\\");\\n        \\n        // Simulate created products\\n        const mockProducts = [\\n          { id: '1', name: 'Premium Tile Set', price: 89.99, image: '\\ud83c\\udff7\\ufe0f' },\\n          { id: '2', name: 'Modern Faucet', price: 149.99, image: '\\ud83d\\udebf' },\\n          { id: '3', name: 'LED Light Fixture', price: 79.99, image: '\\ud83d\\udca1' }\\n        ];\\n        \\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (isMountedRef.current) {\\n            onComplete(mockProducts);\\n          }\\n        }, 1500);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    setTimeout(runStep, 1000);\\n    \\n    return () => {\\n      isMountedRef.current = false;\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\u2699\\ufe0f</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\\n        Processing Your Catalog\\n      </h3>\\n      {fileName && (\\n        <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '16px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n          \\ud83d\\udcc4 {fileName}\\n        </p>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Progress Bar */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n        borderRadius: '10px',\\n        height: '20px',\\n        marginBottom: '8px',\\n        overflow: 'hidden'\\n      }}>\\n        <div style={{\\n          background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${THEME.gold}, ${THEME.goldLight})`,\\n          height: '100%',\\n          width: `${progress}%`,\\n          borderRadius: '10px',\\n          transition: 'width 0.1s linear'\\n        }} />\\n      </div>\\n      <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, fontSize: '0.9em', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        {Math.round(progress)}% \\u2022 {statusText}\\n      </p>\\n\\n      {/* Step List */}\\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'left', maxWidth: '450px', margin: '0 auto 24px' }}>\\n        {STEPS.map((step, idx) => {\\n          const '#4CAF50' : isCurrent ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',\\n                fontSize: isComplete ? '0.9em' : '1.1em',\\n                color: isComplete || isCurrent ? '#fff' : '#666'\\n              }}>\\n                {isComplete ? '\\u2713' : step.icon}\\n              </div>\\n              <span style={{ \\n                color: isComplete ? '#4CAF50' : isCurrent ?
